<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уцелеть.html>уцеле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ucelétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уцелева́ть</b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уцепиться.html>уцепи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ucepítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to catch/lay hold <i>(of)</i>, to seize <i>(on)</i>, to grasp <i>(at)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уцепиться.html>уцепи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ucepítʹsja</b> za predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to catch/jump at a proposal [an offer]</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***участие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:участие.html>уча́стие</a> (1299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:участие.html>уча́стие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učástije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:участие.html>уча́стия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:участие.html>уча́стия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:участие.html>уча́стий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>participation, collaboration, complicity
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>приня́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:участие.html>уча́стие</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prinjátʹ <b>učástije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take part</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>share, stake</li>
<li>sympathy, interest, concern</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:участковый.html>участко́вый</a> (14631)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:участок.html>уча́сток</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učástok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:участковый.html>участко́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učastkóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> division, district</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:участь.html>у́часть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">účastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:участь.html>у́части</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:участь.html>у́части</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:участь.html>у́частей</a></b>)

***учеба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:учеба.html>учёба</a> (4951)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учеба.html>учёба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učóba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учеба.html>учёбы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учеба.html>учёбы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учеба.html>учёб</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>studies, learning
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закончить.html>зако́нчила</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:учеба.html>учёбу</a></strong>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja zakónčila učóbu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I finished my studies. (female speaker)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>study, training, drill</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>че<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́к</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-уч-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-е-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ник</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***ученица.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ученица.html>учени́ца</a> (15286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ученица.html>учени́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učeníca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ученица.html>учени́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ученица.html>учени́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ученица.html>учени́ц</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ученик.html>учени́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>schoolgirl, pupil</li>
<li>pupil, apprentice</li>
<li>disciple, follower</li></ol>

***ученый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ученый.html>учёный</a> (6070)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ёный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jónyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ученый.html>учёный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učónyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)учёнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)учёней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>learned, adept, erudite</li>
<li>scientific, academic</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:учесть.html>уче́сть</a> (2691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:честь.html>честь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учесть.html>уче́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učéstʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учитывать.html>учи́тывать</a></b>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:честь.html>че́сть</a></b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лище</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lišče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:училище.html>учи́лище</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učílišče</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:училище.html>учи́лища</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:училище.html>учи́лища</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:училище.html>учи́лищ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>specialized school, college

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:училище.html>учи́лище</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>učílišče</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at school/college</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:училище.html>учи́лище</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vojénnoje <b>učílišče</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">military school</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">нахи́мовское <b><a href = vnd.unilang:училище.html>учи́лище</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Naxímovskoje <b>učílišče</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Nakhimov Naval School</span></div></dd>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to teach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***учинить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:учинить.html>учини́ть</a> (11967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чинить.html>чини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">činítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учинить.html>учини́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učinítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чинить.html>чини́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учинять.html>учиня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make, to commit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:учинить.html>учини́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скандал.html>сканда́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>učinítʹ</b> skandál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kick up a row</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:учинить.html>учини́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пакость.html>па́кость</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>učinítʹ</b> pákostʹ komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to play a dirty/mean trick on smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:учинить.html>учини́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:расправа.html>распра́ву</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>učinítʹ</b> rasprávu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">inflict reprisals</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>чи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:нить.html>ни́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:учинять.html>учиня́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>у-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-чин-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учителя́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́тели</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учителе́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́телей</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учительница.html>учи́тельница</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Dated.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>teacher, instructor
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́льких</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учителе́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́лся</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U skólʹkix <b>učiteléj</b> ja učílsja!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’ve studied with so many <b>teachers</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>чи́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тель</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 2c(1)  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:основоположник.html>основополо́жник</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учение.html>уче́ния</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 2a <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмах</a> мн. ч.: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́тели</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́телей</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́телям</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́телями</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́телях</a></i>.
</p>
